/****** Object:  View [dbo].[Qry_CustomReport]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE VIEW [dbo].[Qry_CustomReport]
AS
SELECT     *,c.Rep_PathName + '\' +  t.rct_filename as Rep_CompletePathname
FROM         dbo.Rep_Custom C LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Rep_CustomTrn T ON C.Rep_No = T.Rct_RepNo






GO

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[ViewCustomerOutstanding]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE view [dbo].[ViewCustomerOutstanding] As  
 Select PurCompanyId , PurCompanyCount, PurDocno ,PurDocdate ,PurType , PurCustomerId ,isnull(CustomerName,0) as CustomerName ,PurNetAmount- 
 isnull((Select Sum(ReceiptAdjustAmount) From Receipt Where ReceiptRefPurID =PurId Or ReceiptReturnId =PurID ) ,0) As OutstandingAmount  
 from Purchase 
 Left join Customer on Customerid =PurCustomerId  
 Where  PurType in (6,8) 
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[ViewCustomerOutstandingBalance]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:20 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE view [dbo].[ViewCustomerOutstandingBalance] As  
 Select PurCompanyId , PurCompanyCount, PurDocno ,PurDocdate ,PurType , PurCustomerId,isnull(CustomerName,0) as CustomerName ,
PurNetAmount - PurCasHAmount -PurCardAmount -PurUpiAmount -PurCreditNoteAmount -PurReceiptAmount As OutstandingAmount  
 from Purchase 
 Left join Customer on Customerid =PurCustomerId  
 Where  PurType in (6,8) 
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[DeleteGodown]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[DeleteGodown]
    @GodownId BIGINT
AS
BEGIN
    BEGIN TRANSACTION;
    BEGIN TRY
        -- Delete child records in HsnDetails

        -- Delete the header record in Hsn
        DELETE FROM Godown WHERE GodownId = @GodownId;

        -- Commit the transaction if all operations succeed
        COMMIT TRANSACTION;
    END TRY
    BEGIN CATCH
        -- Rollback the transaction in case of any error
        ROLLBACK TRANSACTION;

        -- Return the error details
        DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000), @ErrorSeverity INT, @ErrorState INT;
        SELECT 
            @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),
            @ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),
            @ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();

        RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, @ErrorSeverity, @ErrorState);
    END CATCH
END;
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[DeleteHsn]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
Create Procedure [dbo].[DeleteHsn] 
 @HsnId BIGINT 
 AS 
 BEGIN 
     BEGIN TRANSACTION; 
     BEGIN TRY 
         -- Delete details first 
         DELETE FROM HsnDetails WHERE HsdHsnId = @HsnId; 
         -- Delete header 
         DELETE FROM Hsn WHERE HsnId = @HsnId; 
         COMMIT TRANSACTION; 
     END TRY 
     BEGIN CATCH 
         ROLLBACK TRANSACTION; 
         DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000), @ErrorSeverity INT, @ErrorState INT; 
         SELECT @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(), @ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(), @ErrorState = ERROR_STATE(); 
         RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, @ErrorSeverity, @ErrorState); 
     END CATCH; 
 END 
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[DeleteOrder]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[DeleteOrder]
    @OrdId BIGINT
AS
BEGIN
    BEGIN TRANSACTION;
    BEGIN TRY
        -- Delete child records in OrderTrn
        DELETE FROM OrderTrn WHERE OrdtOrdId = @OrdId;

        -- Delete the header record in OrderTable
        DELETE FROM OrderTable WHERE OrdId = @OrdId;

        -- Commit the transaction if all operations succeed
        COMMIT TRANSACTION;
    END TRY
    BEGIN CATCH
        -- Rollback the transaction in case of any error
        ROLLBACK TRANSACTION;

        -- Return the error details
        DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000), @ErrorSeverity INT, @ErrorState INT;
        SELECT 
            @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),
            @ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),
            @ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();

        RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, @ErrorSeverity, @ErrorState);
    END CATCH
END;
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[DeletePurchase]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[DeletePurchase] 
 @PurId BIGINT   
 AS 
 BEGIN 
 BEGIN TRANSACTION; 
 BEGIN TRY 
 -- Delete child records in HsnDetails 
 Delete From PurchaseChargeTrn Where PurcPurId =@PurId;
 DELETE FROM PurchaseTrn WHERE PurtPurId = @PurId; 
 DELETE FROM Purchase WHERE PurId = @PurId; 
 -- Commit the transaction if all operations succeed 
 COMMIT TRANSACTION; 
 END TRY 
 BEGIN CATCH 
 -- Rollback the transaction in case of any error 
 ROLLBACK TRANSACTION; 
 -- Return the error details 
  DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000), @ErrorSeverity INT, @ErrorState INT; 
 SELECT  
 @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(), 
 @ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(), 
 @ErrorState = ERROR_STATE(); 
    
 RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, @ErrorSeverity, @ErrorState); 
 END CATCH 
 END; 
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[DeleteSize]
    @SizeId BIGINT
AS
BEGIN
    BEGIN TRANSACTION;
    BEGIN TRY
        -- Delete child records in [SizeDetails]
        DELETE FROM [SizeDetails] WHERE [SzdSizeId] = @SizeId;

        -- Delete the header record in [SizeMaster]

        -- Commit the transaction if all operations succeed
        COMMIT TRANSACTION;
    END TRY
    BEGIN CATCH
        -- Rollback the transaction in case of any error
        ROLLBACK TRANSACTION;

        -- Return the error details
        DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000), @ErrorSeverity INT, @ErrorState INT;
        SELECT 
            @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(), 
            @ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(), 
            @ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();

        RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, @ErrorSeverity, @ErrorState);
    END CATCH
END;

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GenerateNewFinancialYearRecord]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GenerateNewFinancialYearRecord]
    @CompanyId BIGINT
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
    
    DECLARE @LatestCompanyId BIGINT;
    DECLARE @NewCompanyId BIGINT;
    DECLARE @CompanyCount VARCHAR(50);
    DECLARE @FinFromDate DATETIME;
    DECLARE @FinToDate DATETIME;
    DECLARE @NewFinFromDate DATETIME;
    DECLARE @NewFinToDate DATETIME;

    -- First, get the CompanyCount for the passed CompanyId
    SELECT @CompanyCount = CompanyCount FROM CompanyProfile WHERE CompanyId = @CompanyId;

    -- If no record is found, exit the procedure
    IF @CompanyCount IS NULL
    BEGIN
        PRINT 'No company record found for the given CompanyId!';
        RETURN;
    END

    -- Then, find the ACTUAL latest record for THIS company (based on CompanyCount)
    SELECT TOP 1 
        @LatestCompanyId = CompanyId,
        @FinFromDate = CompanyFinFromDate,
        @FinToDate = CompanyFinToDate
    FROM CompanyProfile
    WHERE CompanyCount = @CompanyCount
    ORDER BY CompanyFinToDate DESC; 

    -- Calculate new financial year dates
    SET @NewFinFromDate = DATEADD(YEAR, 1, @FinFromDate);
    SET @NewFinToDate = DATEADD(YEAR, 1, @FinToDate);

    -- Check if a record already exists for the new financial year for THIS company
    IF EXISTS (
        SELECT 1 FROM CompanyProfile
        WHERE CompanyCount = @CompanyCount
        AND CompanyFinFromDate = @NewFinFromDate
    )
    BEGIN
        PRINT 'Cannot insert record. A record already exists for this financial year!';
        RETURN;
    END

    -- Generate NEW CompanyId globally (unique across all companies)
    SELECT @NewCompanyId = ISNULL(MAX(CompanyId), 0) + 1 FROM CompanyProfile; 

    -- DYNAMIC SQL TO COPY ALL COLUMNS
    DECLARE @ColumnList NVARCHAR(MAX) = '';
    DECLARE @SelectColumnList NVARCHAR(MAX) = '';

    SELECT 
        @ColumnList += QUOTENAME(name) + ', ',
        @SelectColumnList += CASE 
            WHEN name = 'CompanyId' THEN '@NewCompanyId'
            WHEN name = 'CompanyFinFromDate' THEN '@NewFinFromDate'
            WHEN name = 'CompanyFinToDate' THEN '@NewFinToDate'
            ELSE QUOTENAME(name)
        END + ', '
    FROM sys.columns 
    WHERE object_id = OBJECT_ID('CompanyProfile')
    AND is_computed = 0
    AND is_identity = 0
    AND system_type_id <> 189; -- Exclude timestamp/rowversion

    -- Remove trailing commas
    SET @ColumnList = LEFT(@ColumnList, LEN(@ColumnList) - 1);
    SET @SelectColumnList = LEFT(@SelectColumnList, LEN(@SelectColumnList) - 1);

    -- Construct and execute dynamic SQL
    DECLARE @Sql NVARCHAR(MAX);
    SET @Sql = 'INSERT INTO CompanyProfile (' + @ColumnList + ') ' +
               'SELECT ' + @SelectColumnList + ' ' +
               'FROM CompanyProfile WHERE CompanyId = @LatestCompanyId';

    EXEC sp_executesql @Sql, 
        N'@NewCompanyId BIGINT, @NewFinFromDate DATETIME, @NewFinToDate DATETIME, @LatestCompanyId BIGINT',
        @NewCompanyId, @NewFinFromDate, @NewFinToDate, @LatestCompanyId;

    PRINT 'New financial year record created successfully!';
END;
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetAllCustomers] 
 @CustomerId NUMERIC = NULL, 
 @WhereCond VARCHAR(MAX) = NULL 
 AS 
 BEGIN 
 SET NOCOUNT ON; 
 DECLARE @SQLQuery NVARCHAR(MAX); 
 SET @SQLQuery = N' 
 SELECT  
 CustomerId, 
 CustomerName, 
 CustomerNickName, 
 CustomerAddress1, 
 CustomerAddress2, 
 CustomerAddress3, 
 CustomerEmailID, 
 CustomerMobileNo, 
 CustomerMobileNo2, 
 CustomerGstNo, 
 CustomerPanNo, 
 CustomerBirthDate, 
 CustomerAnnDate, 
 CustomerCityId, 
 CustomerAreaId, 
 CustomerRemarks, 
 CustomerLocation, 
 CustomerMaxPkno, 
 CustomerRecordCreated, 
 CustomerRecordModified, 
 CustomerUserId, 
 CustomerLastModified, 
 CAST(CustomerTimeStamp AS BIGINT) AS CustomerTimeStamp, 
 CustomerDeActive AS ISActive, 
 ISNULL(CustomerGstType, 0) AS CustomerGstType, 
 ISNULL(CustomerCode, '''') AS CustomerCode, 
 ISNULL(CustomerCgid, 0) AS CustomerCgId, 
 ISNULL(CustomerReligionId, 0) AS CustomerReligionId, 
 ISNULL(CustomerPincode, 0) AS CustomerPincode, 
 ISNULL(CustomerGender, 0) AS CustomerGender, 
 Isnull(CustomerIsLedger,0) As CustomerIsLedger 
 FROM Customer WHERE 1=1 '; 
 IF @CustomerId IS NOT NULL 
    SET @SQLQuery = @SQLQuery + ' AND CustomerId = @CustomerId'; 
 IF @WhereCond IS NOT NULL AND @WhereCond <> '' 
    SET @SQLQuery = @SQLQuery + ' ' + @WhereCond; 
 EXEC sp_executesql @SQLQuery, N'@CustomerId NUMERIC', @CustomerId; 
 END;
GO

    SELECT SubSizeId,SubSizeCode, SubSizeName, SubSizeRecordCreated, 
    SubSizeRecordModified, SubSizeUserId, SubSizeLastModified, 
    SubSizeTimestamp,SubSizelocation ,SubSizeMaxPkno,SubSizeIsDefault 
    FROM SubSizeMaster;
END 
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetAllSupplierBrandList]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetAllSupplierBrandList]
                @SupplierId BIGINT = NULL
            AS
            BEGIN
                SET NOCOUNT ON;
                SELECT
                    sbl.SupBrId,
                    sbl.SupbrBrandId,
                    sbl.Supbrlocation,
                    sbl.SupbrMaxPkno,
                    sbl.SupBrSupplierId,
                    sbl.RecordCreated,
                    sbl.RecordModified,
                    sbl.UserId,
                    sbl.LastModified,
                    CAST(sbl.TimeStamp AS BIGINT) AS TimeStamp,
                    b.BrandName
                FROM SupplierBrandList sbl
                LEFT JOIN Brand b ON sbl.SupbrBrandId = b.BrandId
                WHERE (@SupplierId IS NULL OR sbl.SupBrSupplierId = @SupplierId)
                ORDER BY sbl.SupBrId;
            END
GO

Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetAllSuppliers] 
 @SupplierId Numeric =null 
 AS 
 BEGIN 
 SET NOCOUNT ON;
 SELECT  
 SupplierId, 
 SupplierName,
 SupplierNickName,
 SupplierAddress1,
 SupplierAddress2,
 SupplierAddress3,
 SupplierEmailID,
 SupplierMobileNo,
 SupplierMobileNo2,
 SupplierGstNo,
 SupplierPanNo,
 SupplierCityId,
 SupplierAreaId,
 SupplierRemarks,
 SupplierLocation,
 SupplierMaxPkno,
 SupplierRecordCreated,
 SupplierRecordModified,
 SupplierUserId,
 SupplierLastModified, 
 Cast( SupplierTimeStamp as Bigint ) as SupplierTimeStamp, 
 SupplierDeActive As ISActive, 
  isnull(SupplierGstType,0) as SupplierGstType, 
 isnull(SupplierPincode,0) as SupplierPincode , 
 Isnull(SupplierCreditDays,0) As SupplierCreditDays, 
 ISnull(SupplierDiscountPercent, 0) as SupplierDiscountPercent, 
 Isnull(SupplierCode,'') As SupplierCode 
 FROM  
 Supplier 
 Where SupplierId =isnull(@SupplierId,SupplierId);
 END;

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetNextPreviousDate]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetNextPreviousDate] 
( 
  @CurrentDate DATE,
 @Direction CHAR(1) -- 'N' for Next, 'P' for Previous 
 ) 
 AS 
 BEGIN 
 IF @Direction = 'N' 
 BEGIN 
 SELECT TOP 1 ReceiptDocDate 
 FROM Receipt 
 WHERE ReceiptDocDate > @CurrentDate and ReceiptType='3'
 ORDER BY ReceiptDocDate;
 END
 ELSE IF @Direction = 'P'
 BEGIN
 SELECT TOP 1 ReceiptDocDate 
 FROM Receipt 
 WHERE ReceiptDocDate < @CurrentDate  and ReceiptType='3' 
 ORDER BY ReceiptDocDate DESC; 
 END
 END 
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetOrderDetails]
@OrdtOrdID Bigint = NULL
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    SELECT
        OrdtId,
        OrdtOrdId,
        Ordtsdocno,
        OrderBy,
        OrdtSize,
        OrdtDebitQty,
        OrdtCreditQty,
        OrdtBarcodeId,
        OrdtProductId,
        OrdtColorID,
        OrdtRecordCreated,
        OrdtRecordModified,
        OrdtPurchaseRate,
        OrdtSelPrice,
        OrdtMrp,
        OrdtMaxPkno,
        OrdtLocation,
        OrdtHsnId,
        OrdtTaxId,
        OrdtTaxRate1,
        OrdtTaxRate2,
        OrdtDiscountPercent,
        OrdtDiscAmount,
        OrdtSizeId,
        OrdtTaxAmount1,
        OrdtTaxAmount2,
        OrdtDebitAmount,
        OrdtCreditAmount,
        OrdtPerDiscount,
        ISNULL(OrdtRate, OrdtPurchaseRate) AS OrdtRate,
        ISNULL(OrdtParentDocno, 0) AS OrdtParentDocno,
        ISNULL(OrdtParentId, 0) AS OrdtParentId
    FROM
        OrderTrn
    WHERE OrdtOrdId = ISNULL(@OrdtOrdID, OrdtOrdID)
END;

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetPurchaseDetails]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetPurchaseDetails]
@PurtPurID Bigint = NULL
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    SELECT 
        p.PurtId,
        p.PurtPurId,
        p.Purtsdocno,
        p.PurtOrderBy,
        p.PurtSize,
        p.PurtDebitQty,
        p.PurtCreditQty,
        p.PurtBarcodeId,
        p.PurtProductId,
        p.PurtColorID,
        p.PurtRecordCreated,
        p.PurtRecordModified,
        p.PurtPurchaseRate,
        p.PurtSelPrice,
        p.PurtMrp,
        p.PurtMaxPkno,
        p.PurtLocation,
        p.PurtHsnId,
        p.PurtTaxId,
        p.PurtTaxRate1,
        p.PurtTaxRate2,
        p.PurtDiscountPercent,
        p.PurtDiscAmount,
        p.PurtSizeId,
        p.PurtTaxAmount1,
        p.PurtTaxAmount2,
        p.PurtDebitAmount,
        p.PurtCreditAmount,
        p.PurtCostRate,
        ISNULL(p.PurtRate, p.PurtPurchaseRate) AS PurtRate,
        ISNULL(p.PurtParentDocno, 0) AS PurtParentDocno,
        ISNULL(p.PurtParentId, 0) AS PurtParentId,
        ISNULL(p.PurtPerDiscount, 0) AS PurtPerDiscount,
        ISNULL(p.PurtOrdtId, 0) AS PurtOrdtId,
        ISNULL(p.PurtRackNo, 0) AS PurtRackNo,
        Isnull(PurDocNo ,0) as PurtPurchaseDocno ,
        (PurDocdate ) as PurtPurchaseDocdate ,
        isnull(PurOpeningStock,0) as PurOpeningStock,
        ISNULL(p.PurtDetailSDocno, 0) AS PurtDetailSDocno ,
       isnull(p.PurtMiddleRate ,0) As PurtMiddleRate ,
       isnull(p.PurtMiddleMrp, 0) As PurtMiddleMrp ,
       isnull(p.PurtMiddleSelPrice,0) As PurtMiddleSelPrice,
       isnull(p.PurtRateDiff,0) As PurtRateDiff, 
       isnull(p.PurtMrpDiff,0) as PurtMrpDiff,
       isnull(p.PurtMarkdown,0) As PurtMarkDown ,
       isnull(p.PurtMarkDownPercent,0) As PurtMarkDownPercent ,
       isnull(p.PurtSelPriceDiscPercent ,0) As PurtSelPriceDiscPercent,
       isnull(PurCreditBill,0) As PurCreditBill ,
       isnull(PurId ,0) as PurtRefPurId ,
        isnull(p.PurtAlteration,0) as PurtAlteration, 
		isnull(p.PurtSubSizeId,0) as PurtSubSizeId ,
        p.PurtDeliveryDate, 
        p.PurtSalesmanId ,
        isnull(p.PurtRemarks,'') as PurtRemarks ,
        isnull(p.PurtSourcecode,'') as PurtSourcecode, 
        isnull(p.PurtSalesmanPoints,0) as PurtSalesmanPoints 
    FROM 
        PurchaseTrn p 
    Left join PurchaseTrn ref on ref.PurtId =p.PurtParentId 
 Left join Purchase on Purid =ref.PurtPurid 
    WHERE p.PurtPurId =ISnull(@PurtPurId,p.PurtPurID )
END;
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetReceiptRecordsByDate]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[GetReceiptRecordsByDate] 
(
    @Date DATE
)
AS
BEGIN
    SELECT ReceiptId, ReceiptCompanyId, ReceiptCompanyCount, ReceiptType, ReceiptLocation, ReceiptDocno,
           ReceiptDocDate, CustomerId As ReceiptCustomerID, ReceiptAmount, ReceiptAdjustAmount,
           ReceiptRecordCreated, ReceiptRecordModified, ReceiptUserNewId, ReceiptLastModified, ReceiptTimeStamp, ReceiptMaxPkno, ReceiptRefPurID,
           ReceiptAdjustDate, ReceiptPaymentSubTypeId, ReceiptAdvanceId, ReceiptReturnId, ReceiptIsAdvance,
           ISNULL(PaymentSubTypeName, '') AS PaymentSubTypeName,
           ISNULL(PurDocNo, '') AS PurDocNo, PurDocDate,CustomerName,CustomerMobileNo,isnull(PurComments,'') As SalesRemarks  
    FROM Receipt
    LEFT JOIN PaymentSubType ON PaymentSubTypeId = ReceiptPaymentSubTypeId
    LEFT JOIN Purchase ON PurID = ReceiptRefPurID
      LEFT JOIN Customer ON CustomerId =(Case  ReceiptCustomerId When 0 then PurCustomerId Else ReceiptCustomerId End )
    WHERE CONVERT(DATE, ReceiptDocDate) = @Date AND ReceiptType = 3
    ORDER BY ReceiptDocDate, ReceiptId;
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[InsertCountry]
    @CountryName VARCHAR(50),
    @CountryRecordCreated DATETIME,
    @CountryRecordModified DATETIME,
    @CountryUserId BIGINT,
    @CountryLastModified BIGINT,
	@CountryLocation as Bigint ,
	@CountryMaxPkno As Bigint,
	@CountryId As Bigint
AS
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO Country (CountryName ,CountryRecordCreated, CountryRecordModified, CountryUserId, CountryLastModified,Countrylocation ,CountryMaxPkno,Countryid )
    VALUES (@CountryName, @CountryRecordCreated, @CountryRecordModified, @CountryUserId, @CountryLastModified,@CountryLocation,@CountryMaxPkno,@CountryId);
END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[InsertHsn]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[InsertHsn] 
    @HsnCode VARCHAR(30), 
    @HsnDescription VARCHAR(50), 
    @HsnRecordCreated DATETIME, 
    @HsnRecordModified DATETIME, 
    @HsnUserId BIGINT, 
    @HsnLastModified BIGINT, 
    @HsnLocation AS BIGINT, 
    @HsnMaxPkno AS BIGINT, 
    @HsnId AS BIGINT, 
    @HsnDeactive BIT, 
    @HsnWefDate DATE, 
    @HsnWefToDate DATE, 
    @HsnDetails HsnDetailsType READONLY 
AS 
BEGIN 
    SET NOCOUNT ON; 
    DECLARE @CheckId AS BIGINT; 
    BEGIN TRANSACTION; 
    BEGIN TRY 
        -- Insert or Update the header record 
        SELECT @CheckId = HsnId FROM Hsn WHERE HsnId = @HsnId; 
        IF @CheckId IS NULL 
        BEGIN 
            INSERT INTO Hsn (HsnId, HsnCode, HsnDescription, HsnLastModified, HsnLocation, HsnMaxPkno, HsnRecordCreated, HsnRecordModified, HsnUserId, HsnWefDate, HsnWefToDate) 
            VALUES (@HsnId, @HsnCode, @HsnDescription, @HsnLastModified, @HsnLocation, @HsnMaxPkno, @HsnRecordCreated, @HsnRecordModified, @HsnUserId, @HsnWefDate, @HsnWefToDate); 
        END 
        ELSE 
        BEGIN 
            UPDATE Hsn 
            SET HsnDescription = @HsnDescription, HsnCode = @HsnCode, HsnDeactive = @HsnDeactive, 
                HsnWefDate = @HsnWefDate, HsnWefToDate = @HsnWefToDate 
            WHERE HsnId = @HsnId; 
        END 
        -- Insert or Update the details 
        MERGE INTO HsnDetails AS Target 
        USING @HsnDetails AS Source 
        ON Target.HsdId = Source.HsdId 
                WHEN MATCHED THEN 
            UPDATE 
            SET HsdSlabAmount = Source.HsdSlabAmount, 
                HsdSlabTax1 = Source.HsdSlabTax1, 
                HsdSlabTax2 = Source.HsdSlabTax2, 
                HsdRecordModified = Source.HsdRecordModified, 
                HsdUserId = Source.HsdUserId, 
                HsdDeActive = Source.HsdDeActive, 
                HsdHsnId = @HsnId, 
                HsdLocation = Source.HsdLocation, 
                HsdMaxPkno = Source.HsdMaxPkno, 
                HsdLastModified = Source.HsdModified, 
                HsdWefDate = Source.HsdWefDate 
        WHEN NOT MATCHED BY TARGET THEN 
            INSERT (HsdSlabAmount, HsdSlabTax1, HsdSlabTax2, HsdRecordCreated, HsdRecordModified, 
                    HsdUserId, HsdDeActive, HsdHsnId, HsdId, HsdLocation, HsdMaxPkno, HsdLastModified, HsdWefDate) 
            VALUES (Source.HsdSlabAmount, Source.HsdSlabTax1, Source.HsdSlabTax2, Source.HsdRecordCreated, Source.HsdRecordModified, 
                    Source.HsdUserId, Source.HsdDeActive, @HsnId, Source.HsdId, Source.HsdLocation, Source.HsdMaxPkno, Source.HsdModified, Source.HsdWefDate); 
        COMMIT TRANSACTION; 
    END TRY 
    BEGIN CATCH 
        ROLLBACK TRANSACTION; 
 DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000), @ErrorSeverity INT, @ErrorState INT; 
    SELECT @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(), @ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(), @ErrorState = ERROR_STATE(); 
   RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, @ErrorSeverity, @ErrorState);
    END CATCH; 
END;
GO

GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[InsertOrder]
    @OrdCompanyId BIGINT,
    @OrdCompanyCount BIGINT,
    @OrdType BIGINT,
    @OrdLocation BIGINT,
    @OrdDocNo BIGINT,
    @OrdDocDate DATETIME,
    @OrdCustomerId BIGINT,
    @OrdSupplierId BIGINT,
    @OrdGrossAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @OrdDiscountPercent NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @OrdDiscountAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @OrdIgstAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @OrdCgstAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @OrdSgstAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @OrdUgstAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @OrdGstType BIGINT,
    @OrdTcsAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @OrdRecordCreated DATETIME,
    @OrdRecordModified DATETIME,
    @OrdUserNewId BIGINT,
    @OrdLastModified BIGINT,
    @OrdTimeStamp BIGINT,
    @OrdMaxPkno BIGINT,
    @OrdTotalQty NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @OrdBillNo VARCHAR(50),
    @OrdBillDate DATETIME,
    @OrdChallanNo VARCHAR(50),
    @OrdChallanDate DATETIME,
    @OrdId BIGINT,
    @OrdNetAmount DECIMAL(14, 4),
    @OrderDetails OrderDetailsType READONLY
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
    DECLARE @CheckId AS BIGINT;

    BEGIN TRANSACTION;
    BEGIN TRY
        SELECT @CheckId = OrdId FROM [OrderTable] WHERE OrdId = @OrdId;

        IF @CheckId IS NULL
        BEGIN
            INSERT INTO [OrderTable] (
                OrdCompanyId, OrdCompanyCount, OrdType, OrdLocation, OrdDocNo, OrdDocDate,
                OrdCustomerId, OrdGrossAmount, OrdDiscountPercent, OrdDiscountAmount,
                OrdIgstAmount, OrdCgstAmount, OrdSgstAmount, OrdUgstAmount, OrdGstType,
                OrdTcsAmount, OrdRecordCreated, OrdRecordModified, OrdUserNewId,
                OrdLastModified, OrdMaxPkno, OrdTotalQty, OrdBillNo,
                OrdBillDate, OrdChallanNo, OrdChallanDate, OrdId, OrdNetAmount
            )
            VALUES (
                @OrdCompanyId, @OrdCompanyCount, @OrdType, @OrdLocation, @OrdDocNo, @OrdDocDate,
                @OrdCustomerId, @OrdGrossAmount, @OrdDiscountPercent, @OrdDiscountAmount,
                @OrdIgstAmount, @OrdCgstAmount, @OrdSgstAmount, @OrdUgstAmount, @OrdGstType,
                @OrdTcsAmount, @OrdRecordCreated, @OrdRecordModified, @OrdUserNewId,
                @OrdLastModified, @OrdMaxPkno, @OrdTotalQty, @OrdBillNo,
                @OrdBillDate, @OrdChallanNo, @OrdChallanDate, @OrdId, @OrdNetAmount
            );
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
            UPDATE [OrderTable]
            SET
                OrdCompanyId = @OrdCompanyId,
                OrdCompanyCount = @OrdCompanyCount,
                OrdType = @OrdType,
                OrdLocation = @OrdLocation,
                OrdDocNo = @OrdDocNo,
                OrdDocDate = @OrdDocDate,
                OrdCustomerId = @OrdCustomerId,
                OrdGrossAmount = @OrdGrossAmount,
                OrdDiscountPercent = @OrdDiscountPercent,
                OrdDiscountAmount = @OrdDiscountAmount,
                OrdIgstAmount = @OrdIgstAmount,
                OrdCgstAmount = @OrdCgstAmount,
                OrdSgstAmount = @OrdSgstAmount,
                OrdUgstAmount = @OrdUgstAmount,
                OrdGstType = @OrdGstType,
                OrdTcsAmount = @OrdTcsAmount,
                OrdRecordCreated = @OrdRecordCreated,
                OrdRecordModified = @OrdRecordModified,
                OrdUserNewId = @OrdUserNewId,
                OrdLastModified = @OrdLastModified,
                OrdMaxPkno = @OrdMaxPkno,
                OrdTotalQty = @OrdTotalQty,
                OrdBillNo = @OrdBillNo,
                OrdBillDate = @OrdBillDate,
                OrdChallanNo = @OrdChallanNo,
                OrdChallanDate = @OrdChallanDate,
                OrdNetAmount = @OrdNetAmount
            WHERE OrdId = @OrdId;
        END
    -- Merge Order Details
    MERGE INTO OrderTrn AS Target
    USING @OrderDetails AS Source
    ON Target.OrdtId = Source.OrdtId
    WHEN MATCHED THEN
        UPDATE SET
            OrdtOrdId = @OrdId,
            Ordtsdocno = Source.Ordtsdocno,
            OrdtSize = Source.OrdtSize,
            OrdtCreditQty = Source.OrdtCreditQty,
            OrdtBarcodeId = Source.OrdtBarcodeId,
            OrdtProductId = Source.OrdtProductId,
            OrdtColorID = Source.OrdtColorID,
            OrdtRecordModified = Source.OrdtRecordModified,
            OrdtPurchaseRate = Source.OrdtPurchaseRate,
            OrdtSelPrice = Source.OrdtSelPrice,
            OrdtMrp = Source.OrdtMrp,
            OrdtMaxPkno = Source.OrdtMaxPkno,
            OrdtLocation = Source.OrdtLocation,
            OrdtHsnId = Source.OrdtHsnId,
            OrdtTaxId = Source.OrdtTaxId,
            OrdtTaxRate1 = Source.OrdtTaxRate1,
            OrdtTaxRate2 = Source.OrdtTaxRate2,
            OrdtDiscountPercent = Source.OrdtDiscountPercent,
            OrdtDiscAmount = Source.OrdtDiscAmount,
            OrdtSizeId = Source.OrdtSizeId,
            OrdtDebitAmount = Source.OrdtDebitAmount,
            OrdtCreditAmount = Source.OrdtCreditAmount,
            OrdtPerDiscount = Source.OrdtPerDiscount,
            OrdtTaxAmount1 = Source.OrdtTaxAmount1,
            OrdtTaxAmount2 = Source.OrdtTaxAmount2,
            OrdtParentId = Source.OrdtParentId,
            OrdtParentDocno = Source.OrdtParentDocno,
            OrdtRate = Source.OrdtRate
    WHEN NOT MATCHED BY TARGET THEN
        INSERT (
            OrdtId, OrdtOrdId, Ordtsdocno, OrdtSize, OrdtCreditQty,
            OrdtBarcodeId, OrdtProductId, OrdtColorID, OrdtRecordCreated, OrdtRecordModified,
            OrdtPurchaseRate, OrdtSelPrice, OrdtMrp, OrdtMaxPkno, OrdtLocation,
            OrdtHsnId, OrdtTaxId, OrdtTaxRate1, OrdtTaxRate2, OrdtDiscountPercent,
            OrdtDiscAmount, OrdtSizeId, OrdtDebitAmount, OrdtCreditAmount, OrdtPerDiscount,
            OrdtTaxAmount1, OrdtTaxAmount2, OrdtParentId, OrdtParentDocno, OrdtRate
        )
        VALUES (
            Source.OrdtId, @OrdId, Source.Ordtsdocno, Source.OrdtSize,
            Source.OrdtCreditQty, Source.OrdtBarcodeId, Source.OrdtProductId,
            Source.OrdtColorID, Source.OrdtRecordCreated, Source.OrdtRecordModified,
            Source.OrdtPurchaseRate, Source.OrdtSelPrice, Source.OrdtMrp, Source.OrdtMaxPkno,
            Source.OrdtLocation, Source.OrdtHsnId, Source.OrdtTaxId, Source.OrdtTaxRate1,
            Source.OrdtTaxRate2, Source.OrdtDiscountPercent, Source.OrdtDiscAmount,
            Source.OrdtSizeId, Source.OrdtDebitAmount, Source.OrdtCreditAmount,
            Source.OrdtPerDiscount, Source.OrdtTaxAmount1, Source.OrdtTaxAmount2,
            Source.OrdtParentId, Source.OrdtParentDocno, Source.OrdtRate
        );

    COMMIT TRANSACTION;
END TRY
BEGIN CATCH
    ROLLBACK TRANSACTION;
    DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000), @ErrorSeverity INT, @ErrorState INT;
    SELECT
        @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),
        @ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),
        @ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();
    RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, @ErrorSeverity, @ErrorState);
END CATCH;
END;
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[InsertPurchase]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[InsertPurchase]
    @PurCompanyId BIGINT,
    @PurCompanyCount BIGINT,
    @PurType BIGINT,
    @PurLocation BIGINT,
    @PurDocNo BIGINT,
    @PurDocDate DATETIME,
    @PurCustomerId BIGINT,
    @PurSupplierId BIGINT,
    @PurGrossAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @PurDiscountPercent NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @PurDiscountAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @PurIgstAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @PurCgstAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @PurSgstAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @PurUgstAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @PurGstType BIGINT,
    @PurTcsAmount NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @PurRecordCreated DATETIME,
    @PurRecordModified DATETIME,
    @PurUserNewId BIGINT,
    @PurLastModified BIGINT,
    @PurTimeStamp BIGINT,
    @PurMaxPkno BIGINT,
    @PurTotalQty NUMERIC(14, 4),
    @PurBillNo VARCHAR(50),
    @PurBillDate DATETIME,
    @PurChallanNo VARCHAR(50),
    @PurChallanDate DATETIME,
    @PurId BIGINT,
    @PurNetAmount DECIMAL(14,4),
    @PurSalesmanId BIGINT,
    @PurRoundOff DECIMAL(14,4),
    @PurCreditBill BIT,
    @PurExclusiveBill BIT,
    @PurOpeningStock BIT,
    @PurEntryType INT,
    @PurComments VARCHAR(250),
    @PurVerify BIT,
    @PurchaseDetails PurchaseDetailsType READONLY,
    @PurchaseCharges PurchaseChargeType READONLY,
    @OriginalTimeStampBigint BIGINT = NULL,
    @NewTimeStampBigint BIGINT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
    -- NOTE: we won't set XACT_ABORT ON here to preserve outer txns; we manage errors via TRY/CATCH + XACT_STATE()

    DECLARE @startedTran BIT = 0;
    DECLARE @lockResult INT;
    DECLARE @resourceKey NVARCHAR(200);
    DECLARE @startTranCount INT = @@TRANCOUNT;
    SET @resourceKey = N'Sales:' + CONVERT(NVARCHAR(50), @PurId);

    -- Start local transaction only if caller didn't start one
    IF (@@TRANCOUNT = 0)
    BEGIN
        BEGIN TRANSACTION;
        SET @startedTran = 1;
    END
    ELSE
    BEGIN
        SAVE TRANSACTION InsertPurchaseSave;
    END

    BEGIN TRY
        -- Application lock
        EXEC @lockResult = sp_getapplock
            @Resource = @resourceKey,
            @LockMode = N'Exclusive',
            @LockOwner = N'Transaction',
            @LockTimeout = 10000;
        IF (@lockResult < 0) RAISERROR(N'Could not acquire application lock.', 16, 1);

        DECLARE @CheckId BIGINT;
        SELECT @CheckId = PurId FROM Purchase WHERE PurId = @PurId;

        IF @CheckId IS NULL
        BEGIN
            INSERT INTO Purchase
            (
                PurCompanyId, PurCompanyCount, PurType, PurLocation, PurDocNo, PurDocDate,
                PurSupplierId, PurGrossAmount, PurDiscountPercent, PurDiscountAmount,
                PurIgstAmount, PurCgstAmount, PurSgstAmount, PurUgstAmount, PurGstType,
                PurTcsAmount, PurRecordCreated, PurRecordModified, PurUserNewId,
                PurLastModified, PurMaxPkno, PurTotalQty, PurBillNo, PurBillDate, PurChallanNo,
                PurChallanDate, PurId, PurNetAmount, PurCustomerId, PurSalesmanId, PurRoundOff,
                PurCreditBill, PurExclusiveBill, PurOpeningStock, PurEntryType, PurComments, PurVerify
            )
            VALUES
            (
                @PurCompanyId, @PurCompanyCount, @PurType, @PurLocation, @PurDocNo, @PurDocDate,
                @PurSupplierId, @PurGrossAmount, @PurDiscountPercent, @PurDiscountAmount,
                @PurIgstAmount, @PurCgstAmount, @PurSgstAmount, @PurUgstAmount, @PurGstType,
                @PurTcsAmount, @PurRecordCreated, @PurRecordModified, @PurUserNewId,
                @PurLastModified, @PurMaxPkno, @PurTotalQty, @PurBillNo, @PurBillDate, @PurChallanNo,
                @PurChallanDate, @PurId, @PurNetAmount, @PurCustomerId, @PurSalesmanId, @PurRoundOff,
                @PurCreditBill, @PurExclusiveBill, @PurOpeningStock, @PurEntryType, @PurComments, @PurVerify
            );
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
            UPDATE Purchase
               SET PurCompanyId       = @PurCompanyId,
                   PurCompanyCount    = @PurCompanyCount,
                   PurType            = @PurType,
                   PurLocation        = @PurLocation,
                   PurDocNo           = @PurDocNo,
                   PurDocDate         = @PurDocDate,
                   PurSupplierId      = @PurSupplierId,
                   PurCustomerId      = @PurCustomerId,
                   PurGrossAmount     = @PurGrossAmount,
                   PurDiscountPercent = @PurDiscountPercent,
                   PurDiscountAmount  = @PurDiscountAmount,
                   PurIgstAmount      = @PurIgstAmount,
                   PurCgstAmount      = @PurCgstAmount,
                   PurSgstAmount      = @PurSgstAmount,
                   PurUgstAmount      = @PurUgstAmount,
                   PurGstType         = @PurGstType,
                   PurTcsAmount       = @PurTcsAmount,
                   PurRecordCreated   = @PurRecordCreated,
                   PurRecordModified  = @PurRecordModified,
                   PurUserNewId       = @PurUserNewId,
                   PurLastModified    = @PurLastModified,
                   PurMaxPkno         = @PurMaxPkno,
                   PurTotalQty        = @PurTotalQty,
                   PurBillNo          = @PurBillNo,
                   PurBillDate        = @PurBillDate,
                   PurChallanNo       = @PurChallanNo,
                   PurChallanDate     = @PurChallanDate,
                   PurNetAmount       = @PurNetAmount,
                   PurSalesmanId      = @PurSalesmanId,
                   PurRoundOff        = @PurRoundOff,
                   PurCreditBill      = @PurCreditBill,
                   PurExclusiveBill   = @PurExclusiveBill,
                   PurOpeningStock    = @PurOpeningStock,
                   PurEntryType       = @PurEntryType,
                   PurComments        = @PurComments,
                   PurVerify          = @PurVerify
             WHERE PurId = @PurId
               AND ( @OriginalTimeStampBigint IS NULL
                     OR CONVERT(BIGINT, PurTimeStamp) = @OriginalTimeStampBigint );
            IF (@@ROWCOUNT = 0) RAISERROR(N'Concurrency conflict: bill was modified by another user/window.', 16, 1);
        END

        -- Details MERGE
        MERGE INTO PurchaseTrn AS Target
        USING @PurchaseDetails AS Source
           ON Target.PurtId = Source.PurtId
        WHEN MATCHED THEN
            UPDATE SET
                PurtPurId               = @PurId,
                Purtsdocno              = Source.Purtsdocno,
                PurtOrderBy             = Source.PurtOrderBy,
                PurtSize                = Source.PurtSize,
                PurtDebitQty            = Source.PurtDebitQty,
                PurtCreditQty           = Source.PurtCreditQty,
                PurtBarcodeId           = Source.PurtBarcodeId,
                PurtProductId           = Source.PurtProductId,
                PurtColorID             = Source.PurtColorID,
                PurtRecordModified      = Source.PurtRecordModified,
                PurtPurchaseRate        = Source.PurtPurchaseRate,
                PurtSelPrice            = Source.PurtSelPrice,
                PurtMrp                 = Source.PurtMrp,
                PurtMaxPkno             = Source.PurtMaxPkno,
                PurtLocation            = Source.PurtLocation,
                PurtHsnId               = Source.PurtHsnId,
                PurtTaxId               = Source.PurtTaxId,
                PurtTaxRate1            = Source.PurtTaxRate1,
                PurtTaxRate2            = Source.PurtTaxRate2,
                PurtDiscountPercent     = Source.PurtDiscountPercent,
                PurtDiscAmount          = Source.PurtDiscAmount,
                PurtSizeId              = Source.PurtSizeId,
                PurtCostRate            = Source.PurtCostRate,
                PurtDebitAmount         = Source.PurtDebitAmount,
                PurtCreditAmount        = Source.PurtCreditAmount,
                PurtPerQty              = Source.PurtPerQty,
                PurtPerDiscount         = Source.PurtPerDiscount,
                PurtTaxAmount1          = Source.PurtTaxAmount1,
                PurtTaxAmount2          = Source.PurtTaxAmount2,
                PurtRate                = Source.PurtRate,
                PurtParentId            = Source.PurtParentId,
                PurtParentDocno         = Source.PurtParentDocno,
                PurtOrdtId              = Source.PurtOrdtId,
                PurtRackNo              = Source.PurtRackNo,
                PurtDetailSDocno        = Source.PurtDetailSDocno,
                PurtMiddleRate          = Source.PurtMiddleRate,
                PurtMiddleMrp           = Source.PurtMiddleMrp,
                PurtMiddleSelPrice      = Source.PurtMiddleSelPrice,
                PurtSizeFrom            = Source.PurtSizeFrom,
                PurtSizeTo              = Source.PurtSizeTo,
                PurtSizeMiddle          = Source.PurtSizeMiddle,
                PurtSelPriceDiscPercent = Source.PurtSelPriceDiscPercent,
                PurtRateDiff            = Source.PurtRateDiff,
                PurtMrpDiff             = Source.PurtMrpDiff,
                PurtMarkDown            = Source.PurtMarkDown,
                PurtMarkDownPercent     = Source.PurtMarkDownPercent,
                PurtAlteration          = Source.PurtAlteration,
                PurtSubSizeId           = Source.PurtSubSizeId,
                PurtDeliveryDate        = Source.PurtDeliveryDate,
                PurtSalesmanId          = Source.PurtSalesmanId,
                PurtRemarks             = Source.PurtRemarks,
                Target.PurtSalesmanPoints    = Source.PurtSalesmanPoints,
                Target.PurtTotalSalesmanpoint    = Source.PurtTotalSalesmanpoint,
                PurtSourcecode          = Source.PurtSourcecode
        WHEN NOT MATCHED BY TARGET THEN
            INSERT
            (
                PurtId, PurtPurId, Purtsdocno, PurtOrderBy, PurtSize, PurtDebitQty, PurtCreditQty,
                PurtBarcodeId, PurtProductId, PurtColorID, PurtRecordCreated, PurtRecordModified,
                PurtPurchaseRate, PurtSelPrice, PurtMrp, PurtMaxPkno, PurtLocation,
                PurtHsnId, PurtTaxId, PurtTaxRate1, PurtTaxRate2, PurtDiscountPercent,
                PurtDiscAmount, PurtSizeId, PurtDebitAmount, PurtCreditAmount, PurtPerQty,
                PurtPerDiscount, PurtCostRate, PurtTaxAmount1, PurtTaxAmount2, PurtParentId,
                PurtParentDocno, PurtRate, PurtOrdtId, PurtRackNo, PurtDetailSDocno,
                PurtMiddleRate, PurtMiddleMrp, PurtMiddleSelPrice, PurtSizeFrom, PurtSizeTo,
                PurtSizeMiddle, PurtSelPriceDiscPercent, PurtRateDiff, PurtMrpDiff,
                PurtMarkDown, PurtMarkDownPercent, PurtAlteration, PurtSubSizeId, PurtDeliveryDate,
                PurtSalesmanId, PurtRemarks, PurtSourcecode, PurtSalesmanPoints, PurtTotalSalesmanpoint 
            )
            VALUES
            (
                Source.PurtId, @PurId, Source.Purtsdocno, Source.PurtOrderBy, Source.PurtSize, Source.PurtDebitQty, Source.PurtCreditQty,
                Source.PurtBarcodeId, Source.PurtProductId, Source.PurtColorID, Source.PurtRecordCreated, Source.PurtRecordModified,
                Source.PurtPurchaseRate, Source.PurtSelPrice, Source.PurtMrp, Source.PurtMaxPkno, Source.PurtLocation,
                Source.PurtHsnId, Source.PurtTaxId, Source.PurtTaxRate1, Source.PurtTaxRate2, Source.PurtDiscountPercent,
                Source.PurtDiscAmount, Source.PurtSizeId, Source.PurtDebitAmount, Source.PurtCreditAmount, Source.PurtPerQty,
                Source.PurtPerDiscount, Source.PurtCostRate, Source.PurtTaxAmount1, Source.PurtTaxAmount2, Source.PurtParentId,
                Source.PurtParentDocno, Source.PurtRate, Source.PurtOrdtId, Source.PurtRackNo, Source.PurtDetailSDocno,
                Source.PurtMiddleRate, Source.PurtMiddleMrp, Source.PurtMiddleSelPrice, Source.PurtSizeFrom, Source.PurtSizeTo,
                Source.PurtSizeMiddle, Source.PurtSelPriceDiscPercent, Source.PurtRateDiff, Source.PurtMrpDiff,
                Source.PurtMarkDown, Source.PurtMarkDownPercent, Source.PurtAlteration, Source.PurtSubSizeId, Source.PurtDeliveryDate,
                Source.PurtSalesmanId, Source.PurtRemarks, Source.PurtSourcecode, Source.PurtSalesmanPoints, Source.PurtTotalSalesmanpoint 
            );

        -- Charges MERGE
        MERGE INTO PurchaseChargeTrn AS Target
        USING @PurchaseCharges AS Source
           ON Target.PurcId = Source.PurcId
        WHEN MATCHED THEN
            UPDATE SET
                Target.PurcPurId             = @PurId,
                Target.PurcChargeId          = Source.PurcChargeId,
                Target.PurcChargeRate        = Source.PurcChargeRate,
                Target.PurcAmount            = Source.PurcAmount,
                Target.PurcTaxId             = Source.PurcTaxId,
                Target.PurcTaxRate1          = Source.PurcTaxRate1,
                Target.PurcTaxAmount1        = Source.PurcTaxAmount1,
                Target.PurcTaxRate2          = Source.PurcTaxRate2,
                Target.PurcTaxAmount2        = Source.PurcTaxAmount2,
                Target.PurcRecordModified    = Source.PurcRecordModified,
                Target.PurcMaxPkno           = Source.PurcMaxPkno,
                Target.PurcLocation          = Source.PurcLocation,
                Target.PurcHsnId             = Source.PurcHsnId,
                Target.PurcReverseTaxAmount1 = Source.PurcReverseTaxAmount1,
                Target.PurcReverseTaxAmount2 = Source.PurcReverseTaxAmount2
        WHEN NOT MATCHED BY TARGET THEN
            INSERT
            (
                PurcId, PurcPurId, PurcChargeId, PurcChargeRate, PurcAmount,
                PurcTaxId, PurcTaxRate1, PurcTaxAmount1, PurcTaxRate2,
                PurcTaxAmount2, PurcRecordCreated, PurcRecordModified,
                PurcMaxPkno, PurcLocation, PurcHsnId,
                PurcReverseTaxAmount1, PurcReverseTaxAmount2
            )
            VALUES
            (
                Source.PurcId, @PurId, Source.PurcChargeId, Source.PurcChargeRate, Source.PurcAmount,
                Source.PurcTaxId, Source.PurcTaxRate1, Source.PurcTaxAmount1, Source.PurcTaxRate2,
                Source.PurcTaxAmount2, Source.PurcRecordCreated, Source.PurcRecordModified,
                Source.PurcMaxPkno, Source.PurcLocation, Source.PurcHsnId,
                Source.PurcReverseTaxAmount1, Source.PurcReverseTaxAmount2
            );

        -- Return fresh timestamp
        SELECT @NewTimeStampBigint = CONVERT(BIGINT, PurTimeStamp)
          FROM Purchase WHERE PurId = @PurId;

        -- Commit only if we started the transaction
        IF (@startedTran = 1 AND @@TRANCOUNT > 0) COMMIT TRANSACTION;
    END TRY
    BEGIN CATCH
        -- Rollback logic that preserves outer transaction
        IF (XACT_STATE() <> 0)
        BEGIN
            IF (@startedTran = 1)
            BEGIN
                IF (@@TRANCOUNT > 0) ROLLBACK TRANSACTION;
            END
            ELSE
            BEGIN
                IF (@@TRANCOUNT > 0) ROLLBACK TRANSACTION InsertPurchaseSave;
            END
        END
        DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000), @ErrorSeverity INT, @ErrorState INT;
        SELECT  @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),
                @ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),
                @ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();
        RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, 16, 1);
    END CATCH
END;
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[InsertSize]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[InsertSize]
     @SizeCode VARCHAR(30),
    @SizeDescription VARCHAR(50),
    @SizeRecordCreated DATETIME,
    @SizeRecordModified DATETIME,
    @SizeUserId BIGINT,
    @SizeLastModified BIGINT,
    @SizeLocation AS BIGINT,
    @SizeMaxPkno AS BIGINT,
    @SizeId AS BIGINT,
    @SizeDeactive BIT,
    @SizeDetails SizeDetailsType READONLY
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
    DECLARE @CheckId AS BIGINT;
    BEGIN TRANSACTION;
    BEGIN TRY
        -- Insert or Update the header record

        -- Check if a Size record with the same SizeCode exists
        SELECT @CheckId = SizeId FROM SizeMaster WHERE SizeId = @SizeId;

        IF @CheckId IS NULL
        BEGIN
            -- Insert new Size record
            INSERT INTO SizeMaster (SizeId, SizeCode, SizeDescription, SizeLastModified, SizeLocation, SizeMaxPkno, SizeRecordCreated, SizeRecordModified, SizeUserId)
            VALUES (@SizeId, @SizeCode, @SizeDescription, @SizeLastModified, @SizeLocation, @SizeMaxPkno, @SizeRecordCreated, @SizeRecordModified, @SizeUserId);
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
            -- Update existing Size record
            UPDATE SizeMaster
            SET SizeDescription = @SizeDescription, SizeCode = @SizeCode, SizeDeactive = @SizeDeactive
            WHERE SizeId = @SizeId;
        END

        -- Insert or Update the details
        MERGE INTO SizeDetails AS Target
        USING @SizeDetails AS Source
        ON Target.SzdId = Source.SzdId -- Match based on existing SzdId
        WHEN MATCHED THEN
            UPDATE
            SET
                SzdAddtionalDetail = Source.SzdAddtionalDetail,
                SzdSize = Source.SzdSize,
                SzdOrderBy = Source.SzdOrderBy,
                SzdRecordModified = Source.SzdRecordModified,
                SzdUserId = Source.SzdUserId,
                SzdDeActive = Source.SzdDeActive,
                SzdSizeId = @SizeId, -- Explicitly assign the parent SizeId
                SzdLocation = Source.SzdLocation,
                SzdMaxPkno = Source.SzdMaxPkno,
                SzdLastModified = Source.SzdModified
        WHEN NOT MATCHED BY TARGET THEN
            INSERT (
                SzdSize, SzdAddtionalDetail, SzdOrderBy,
                SzdRecordCreated, SzdRecordModified,
                SzdUserId, SzdDeActive, SzdSizeId, SzdId, SzdLocation, SzdMaxPkno, SzdLastModified
            )
            VALUES (
                Source.SzdSize, Source.SzdAddtionalDetail, Source.SzdOrderBy,
                Source.SzdRecordCreated, Source.SzdRecordModified,
                Source.SzdUserId, Source.SzdDeActive, @SizeId, -- Assign @SizeId explicitly to SzdSizeId
                Source.SzdId, Source.SzdLocation, Source.SzdMaxPkno, Source.SzdModified
            );

        COMMIT TRANSACTION;
    END TRY
    BEGIN CATCH
        ROLLBACK TRANSACTION;
  DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000), @ErrorSeverity INT, @ErrorState INT; 
 SELECT  
 @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(), 
 @ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(), 
 @ErrorState = ERROR_STATE(); 
  RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, @ErrorSeverity, @ErrorState); 
    END CATCH;
END;
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SaveCustomer]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveCustomer]
    @CustomerXML XML,
    @CustomerNew BIT,
    @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000) OUTPUT 
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    DECLARE @Customer TABLE (
        CustomerId INT,
        CustomerName NVARCHAR(50),
        CustomerNickName NVARCHAR(50),
        CustomerAddress1 NVARCHAR(100),
        CustomerAddress2 NVARCHAR(100),
        CustomerAddress3 NVARCHAR(100),
        CustomerEmailID NVARCHAR(100),
        CustomerMobileNo NVARCHAR(20),
        CustomerMobileNo2 NVARCHAR(20),
        CustomerGstNo NVARCHAR(20),
        CustomerPanNo NVARCHAR(20),
        CustomerBirthDate DATE,
        CustomerAnnDate DATE,
        CustomerCityId INT,
        CustomerAreaId INT,
        CustomerRemarks NVARCHAR(200),
        CustomerLocation INT,
        CustomerMaxPkno INT,
        CustomerRecordCreated DATETIME,
        CustomerRecordModified DATETIME,
        CustomerUserId INT,
        CustomerLastModified INT,
        CustomerTimeStamp INT,
        CustomerDeActive BIT,
        CustomerCode NVARCHAR(20) ,
        CustomerPincode INT , 
        CustomerCgId int , 
        CustomerReligionId int,  
        CustomerGender int, 
        CustomerGstType int ,
        CustomerIsLedger Bit 
    )

     INSERT INTO @Customer
    SELECT
        x.c.value('(CustomerId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerName)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(50)'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerNickName)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(50)'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerAddress1)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(100)'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerAddress2)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(100)'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerAddress3)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(100)'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerEmailID)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(100)'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerMobileNo)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20)'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerMobileNo2)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20)'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerGstNo)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20)'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerPanNo)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20)'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerBirthDate)[1]', 'DATE'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerAnnDate)[1]', 'DATE'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerCityId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerAreaId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerRemarks)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(200)'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerLocation)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerMaxPkno)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerRecordCreated)[1]', 'DATETIME'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerRecordModified)[1]', 'DATETIME'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerUserId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerLastModified)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerTimeStamp)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerDeActive)[1]', 'BIT'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerCode)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20) '),
        x.c.value('(CustomerPincode)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerCgId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerReligionId)[1]', 'Int'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerGender)[1]', 'Int'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerGstType)[1]', 'Int'),
        x.c.value('(CustomerIsLedger)[1]', 'Bit')
    FROM @CustomerXML.nodes('/customer') x(c);


    BEGIN TRY
        IF @CustomerNew = 1
        BEGIN
            INSERT INTO Customer (
                CustomerName,
                CustomerNickName,
                CustomerAddress1,
                CustomerAddress2,
                CustomerAddress3,
                CustomerEmailID,
                CustomerMobileNo,
                CustomerMobileNo2,
                CustomerGstNo,
                CustomerPanNo,
                CustomerBirthDate,
                CustomerAnnDate,
                CustomerCityId,
                CustomerAreaId,
                CustomerRemarks,
                CustomerLocation,
                CustomerMaxPkno,
                CustomerRecordCreated,
                CustomerRecordModified,
                CustomerUserId,
                CustomerLastModified,
                CustomerDeActive,
                CustomerId ,
                CustomerCode ,
                CustomerPincode,
                CustomerCgId,
                CustomerReligionId,
                CustomerGender,
                CustomerGstType,
                CustomerIsLedger

            )
            SELECT
                CustomerName,
                CustomerNickName,
                CustomerAddress1,
                CustomerAddress2,
                CustomerAddress3,
                CustomerEmailID,
                CustomerMobileNo,
                CustomerMobileNo2,
                CustomerGstNo,
                CustomerPanNo,
                CustomerBirthDate,
                CustomerAnnDate,
                CustomerCityId,
                CustomerAreaId,
                CustomerRemarks,
                CustomerLocation,
                CustomerMaxPkno,
                CustomerRecordCreated,
                CustomerRecordModified,
                CustomerUserId,
                CustomerLastModified,
                CustomerDeActive,
                CustomerId,
                CustomerCode, 
                CustomerPincode, 
                CustomerCgId,
                CustomerReligionId,
                CustomerGender,
                CustomerGstType,
                CustomerIsLedger

            FROM @Customer;
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
            DECLARE @ExistingTimeStamp INT;

            SELECT @ExistingTimeStamp = CustomerTimeStamp
            FROM Customer
            WHERE CustomerId = (SELECT CustomerId FROM @Customer);

            IF @ExistingTimeStamp IS NULL
            BEGIN
                SET @ErrorMessage = 'Customer record not found.';
                RETURN;
            END

            IF @ExistingTimeStamp != (SELECT CustomerTimeStamp FROM @Customer)
            BEGIN
                SET @ErrorMessage = 'The record has been modified by another user.';
                RETURN;
            END

            UPDATE Customer
            SET
                CustomerName = c.CustomerName,
                CustomerNickName = c.CustomerNickName,
                CustomerAddress1 = c.CustomerAddress1,
                CustomerAddress2 = c.CustomerAddress2,
                CustomerAddress3 = c.CustomerAddress3,
                CustomerEmailID = c.CustomerEmailID,
                CustomerMobileNo = c.CustomerMobileNo,
                CustomerMobileNo2 = c.CustomerMobileNo2,
                CustomerGstNo = c.CustomerGstNo,
                CustomerPanNo = c.CustomerPanNo,
                CustomerBirthDate = c.CustomerBirthDate,
                CustomerAnnDate = c.CustomerAnnDate,
                CustomerCityId = c.CustomerCityId,
                CustomerAreaId = c.CustomerAreaId,
                CustomerRemarks = c.CustomerRemarks,
                CustomerLocation = c.CustomerLocation,
                CustomerMaxPkno = c.CustomerMaxPkno,
                CustomerRecordModified = c.CustomerRecordModified,
                CustomerUserId = c.CustomerUserId,
                CustomerLastModified = c.CustomerLastModified,
                CustomerDeActive = c.CustomerDeActive , 
                CustomerCode = c.CustomerCode, 
                CustomerPincode=c.CustomerPincode,
                CustomerReligionId=c.CustomerReligionId,
                CustomerCgId=c.CustomerCgid,
                CustomerGender=c.CustomerGender,
                CustomerGstType=c.CustomerGstType,
                CustomerIsLedger=c.CustomerIsLedger
            FROM @Customer c
            WHERE Customer.CustomerId = c.CustomerId;
        END

        SET @ErrorMessage = NULL;
    END TRY
    BEGIN CATCH
        -- Capture and return the error message
        SET @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE();
            END CATCH 
END; 
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SaveExpenseRecord]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveExpenseRecord]
    @ReceiptId BIGINT = 0,
    @ReceiptCompanyId BIGINT,
    @ReceiptLocation BIGINT,
    @ReceiptDocDate DATETIME,
    @ReceiptDocNo VARCHAR(50),
    @ReceiptAmount DECIMAL(18,2),
    @ReceiptPaymentSubTypeId BIGINT,
    @ReceiptLedgerId BIGINT,
    @ReceiptIsExpense BIT,
    @ReceiptDirection TINYINT,
    @ReceiptNotes NVARCHAR(500) = '',
    @UserId BIGINT
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
    
    IF @ReceiptId = 0
    BEGIN
        -- Insert new record
        INSERT INTO Receipt (
            ReceiptCompanyId, ReceiptLocation, ReceiptDocDate, ReceiptDocNo, 
            ReceiptAmount, ReceiptPaymentSubTypeId, ReceiptLedgerId, ReceiptIsExpense,
            ReceiptDirection, ReceiptNotes, ReceiptRecordCreated, ReceiptRecordModified,
            ReceiptUserNewId, ReceiptLastModified, ReceiptType
        )
        VALUES (
            @ReceiptCompanyId, @ReceiptLocation, @ReceiptDocDate, @ReceiptDocNo,
            @ReceiptAmount, @ReceiptPaymentSubTypeId, @ReceiptLedgerId, @ReceiptIsExpense,
            @ReceiptDirection, @ReceiptNotes, GETDATE(), GETDATE(),
            @UserId, @UserId, 4 -- 4 for Daily Expense
        );
        
        SELECT SCOPE_IDENTITY() AS ReceiptId;
    END
    ELSE
    BEGIN
        -- Update existing record
        UPDATE Receipt SET
            ReceiptCompanyId = @ReceiptCompanyId,
            ReceiptLocation = @ReceiptLocation,
            ReceiptDocDate = @ReceiptDocDate,
            ReceiptDocNo = @ReceiptDocNo,
            ReceiptAmount = @ReceiptAmount,
            ReceiptPaymentSubTypeId = @ReceiptPaymentSubTypeId,
            ReceiptLedgerId = @ReceiptLedgerId,
            ReceiptIsExpense = @ReceiptIsExpense,
            ReceiptDirection = @ReceiptDirection,
            ReceiptNotes = @ReceiptNotes,
            ReceiptRecordModified = GETDATE(),
            ReceiptLastModified = @UserId
        WHERE ReceiptId = @ReceiptId;
        
        SELECT @ReceiptId AS ReceiptId;
    END
END
GO

Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveJobber]
    @JobberXML XML,
    @JobberNew BIT,  
    @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000) OUTPUT  
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    DECLARE @Jobber TABLE (
        JobberId INT,
        JobberName NVARCHAR(50),
        JobberNickName NVARCHAR(50),
        JobberAddress1 NVARCHAR(100),
        JobberAddress2 NVARCHAR(100),
        JobberAddress3 NVARCHAR(100),
        JobberEmailID NVARCHAR(100),
        JobberMobileNo NVARCHAR(20),
        JobberMobileNo2 NVARCHAR(20),
        JobberGstNo NVARCHAR(20),
        JobberPanNo NVARCHAR(20),
        JobberCityId INT,
        JobberAreaId INT,
        JobberRemarks NVARCHAR(200),
        JobberLocation INT,
        JobberMaxPkno INT,
        JobberRecordCreated DATETIME,
        JobberRecordModified DATETIME,
        JobberUserId INT,
        JobberLastModified INT,        JobberTimeStamp INT,
        JobberDeActive BIT,
 JobberGstType int,
 JobberPincode int ,
 JobberCreditDays int ,
 JobberDiscountPercent Decimal(14,4), 
 JobberCode varchar(20) 
    )     INSERT INTO @Jobber
    SELECT
        x.c.value('(JobberId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(JobberName)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(50)'),
        x.c.value('(JobberNickName)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(50)'),
        x.c.value('(JobberAddress1)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(100)'),
        x.c.value('(JobberAddress2)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(100)'),
        x.c.value('(JobberAddress3)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(100)'),
        x.c.value('(JobberEmailID)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(100)'),
        x.c.value('(JobberMobileNo)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20)'),
        x.c.value('(JobberMobileNo2)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20)'),
        x.c.value('(JobberGstNo)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20)'),
        x.c.value('(JobberPanNo)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20)'),
        x.c.value('(JobberCityId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(JobberAreaId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(JobberRemarks)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(200)'),
        x.c.value('(JobberLocation)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(JobberMaxPkno)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(JobberRecordCreated)[1]', 'DATETIME'),
        x.c.value('(JobberRecordModified)[1]', 'DATETIME'),
        x.c.value('(JobberUserId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(JobberLastModified)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(JobberTimeStamp)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(JobberDeActive)[1]', 'BIT'),
       x.c.value('(JobberGstType)[1]', 'INT'), 
       x.c.value('(JobberPincode)[1]', 'INT'), 
       x.c.value('(JobberCreditDays)[1]', 'INT'), 
       x.c.value('(JobberDiscountPercent)[1]', 'Decimal(14,4)'), 
       x.c.value('(JobberCode)[1]', 'varchar(20)') 
    FROM @JobberXML.nodes('/Jobber') x(c);


    BEGIN TRY
        IF @JobberNew = 1
        BEGIN
            INSERT INTO Jobber (
                JobberName,
                JobberNickName,
                JobberAddress1,
                JobberAddress2,
                JobberAddress3,
                JobberEmailID,
                JobberMobileNo,
                JobberMobileNo2,
                JobberGstNo,
                JobberPanNo,
                JobberCityId,
                JobberAreaId,
                JobberRemarks,
                JobberLocation,
                JobberMaxPkno,
                JobberRecordCreated,
                JobberRecordModified,
                JobberUserId,
                JobberLastModified,
                JobberDeActive,
                JobberId,
                JobberGstType ,
                JobberPincode, 
                JobberCreditDays, 
                JobberDiscountPercent, 
                JobberCode 

            )
            SELECT
                JobberName,
                JobberNickName,
                JobberAddress1,
                JobberAddress2,
                JobberAddress3,
                JobberEmailID,
                JobberMobileNo,
                JobberMobileNo2,
                JobberGstNo,
                JobberPanNo,
                JobberCityId,
                JobberAreaId,
          JobberRemarks,
                JobberLocation,
                JobberMaxPkno,
                JobberRecordCreated,
                JobberRecordModified,
                JobberUserId,
                JobberLastModified,
                JobberDeActive,
                JobberId,
                JobberGstType, 
               JobberPincode, 
               JobberCreditDays, 
               JobberDiscountPercent, 
               JobberCode 

            FROM @Jobber;
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
            DECLARE @ExistingTimeStamp INT;

            SELECT @ExistingTimeStamp = JobberTimeStamp
            FROM Jobber
            WHERE JobberId = (SELECT JobberId FROM @Jobber);

            IF @ExistingTimeStamp IS NULL
            BEGIN
                SET @ErrorMessage = 'Jobber record not found.';
                RETURN;
            END

            IF @ExistingTimeStamp != (SELECT JobberTimeStamp FROM @Jobber)
            BEGIN
                SET @ErrorMessage = 'The record has been modified by another user.';
                RETURN;
            END

            UPDATE Jobber
            SET
                JobberName = c.JobberName,
                JobberNickName = c.JobberNickName,
                JobberAddress1 = c.JobberAddress1,
                JobberAddress2 = c.JobberAddress2,
                JobberAddress3 = c.JobberAddress3,
                JobberEmailID = c.JobberEmailID,
                JobberMobileNo = c.JobberMobileNo,
                JobberMobileNo2 = c.JobberMobileNo2,
                JobberGstNo = c.JobberGstNo,
                JobberPanNo = c.JobberPanNo,
                JobberCityId = c.JobberCityId,
                JobberAreaId = c.JobberAreaId,
                JobberRemarks = c.JobberRemarks,
                JobberLocation = c.JobberLocation,
                JobberMaxPkno = c.JobberMaxPkno,
                JobberRecordModified = c.JobberRecordModified,
                JobberUserId = c.JobberUserId,
                JobberLastModified = c.JobberLastModified,
                JobberDeActive = c.JobberDeActive ,
   			 JobberGstType =c.JobberGstType, 
                JobberPincode =c.JobberPincode, 
                JobberDiscountPercent =c.JobberDiscountPercent,
                JobberCreditDays =c.JobberCreditDays, 
                JobberCode =c.JobberCode  
            FROM @Jobber c
            WHERE Jobber.JobberId = c.JobberId;
        END

        SET @ErrorMessage = NULL;
    END TRY
    BEGIN CATCH
        -- Capture and return the error message
        SET @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE();
         END CATCH   END; 
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveReceiptRecord] 
(
    @ReceiptId INT,
    @ReceiptCompanyId INT,
    @ReceiptCompanyCount INT,
    @ReceiptType VARCHAR(50),
    @ReceiptLocation VARCHAR(100),
    @ReceiptDocno VARCHAR(50),
    @ReceiptDocDate DATE,
    @ReceiptCustomerId INT,
    @ReceiptAmount DECIMAL(18, 2),
    @ReceiptAdjustAmount DECIMAL(18, 2),
    @ReceiptRecordCreated DATETIME,
    @ReceiptRecordModified DATETIME,
    @ReceiptUserNewId INT,
    @ReceiptLastModified INT,
    @ReceiptMaxPkno INT,
    @ReceiptRefPurID INT,
    @ReceiptAdjustDate DATE,
    @ReceiptPaymentSubTypeId INT,
    @ReceiptAdvanceId BIGINT,
    @ReceiptReturnId BIGINT,
    @ReceiptIsAdvance BIT
)
AS
BEGIN
    IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM Receipt WHERE ReceiptId = @ReceiptId)
    BEGIN
        UPDATE Receipt
        SET ReceiptCompanyId = @ReceiptCompanyId,
            ReceiptCompanyCount = @ReceiptCompanyCount,
            ReceiptType = @ReceiptType,
            ReceiptLocation = @ReceiptLocation,
            ReceiptDocno = @ReceiptDocno,
            ReceiptDocDate = @ReceiptDocDate,
            ReceiptCustomerId = @ReceiptCustomerId,
            ReceiptAmount = @ReceiptAmount,
            ReceiptAdjustAmount = @ReceiptAdjustAmount,
            ReceiptRecordModified = @ReceiptRecordModified,
            ReceiptUserNewId = @ReceiptUserNewId,
            ReceiptLastModified = @ReceiptLastModified,
            ReceiptMaxPkno = @ReceiptMaxPkno,
            ReceiptRefPurID = @ReceiptRefPurID,
            ReceiptAdjustDate = @ReceiptAdjustDate,
            ReceiptPaymentSubTypeId = @ReceiptPaymentSubTypeId,
            ReceiptAdvanceId = @ReceiptAdvanceId,
            ReceiptReturnId = @ReceiptReturnId,
            ReceiptIsAdvance = @ReceiptIsAdvance
        WHERE ReceiptId = @ReceiptId;
    END
    ELSE
    BEGIN
        INSERT INTO Receipt (
            ReceiptCompanyId, ReceiptCompanyCount, ReceiptType, ReceiptLocation, ReceiptDocno,
            ReceiptDocDate, ReceiptCustomerId, ReceiptAmount, ReceiptAdjustAmount, ReceiptRecordCreated,
            ReceiptUserNewId, ReceiptMaxPkno, ReceiptRefPurID, ReceiptAdjustDate,
            ReceiptPaymentSubTypeId, ReceiptAdvanceId, ReceiptReturnId, ReceiptIsAdvance, ReceiptId
        )
        VALUES (
            @ReceiptCompanyId, @ReceiptCompanyCount, @ReceiptType, @ReceiptLocation, @ReceiptDocno,
            @ReceiptDocDate, @ReceiptCustomerId, @ReceiptAmount, @ReceiptAdjustAmount, @ReceiptRecordCreated,
            @ReceiptUserNewId, @ReceiptMaxPkno, @ReceiptRefPurID, @ReceiptAdjustDate,
            @ReceiptPaymentSubTypeId, @ReceiptAdvanceId, @ReceiptReturnId, @ReceiptIsAdvance, @ReceiptId
        );
    END
END
GO

                SalesmanDeActive = c.SalesmanDeActive  ,
SalesmanCommission=c.SalesmanCommission,
SalesmanCode=c.SalesmanCode
            FROM @Salesman c
            WHERE Salesman.SalesmanId = c.SalesmanId;
        END

        SET @ErrorMessage = NULL;

    BEGIN CATCH

        SET @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE();

Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveSupplier]

AS
BEGIN

    DECLARE @Supplier TABLE (
        SupplierId INT,

        SupplierAddress2 NVARCHAR(100),

        SupplierEmailID NVARCHAR(100),
        SupplierMobileNo NVARCHAR(20),
        SupplierMobileNo2 NVARCHAR(20),
        SupplierGstNo NVARCHAR(20),
        SupplierPanNo NVARCHAR(20),
        SupplierCityId INT,
        SupplierAreaId INT,
        SupplierRemarks NVARCHAR(200),
        SupplierLocation INT,
        SupplierMaxPkno INT,
        SupplierRecordCreated DATETIME,
        SupplierRecordModified DATETIME,
        SupplierUserId INT,
        SupplierLastModified INT,        SupplierTimeStamp INT,
        SupplierDeActive BIT,
 SupplierGstType int,
 SupplierPincode int ,
 SupplierCreditDays int ,
 SupplierDiscountPercent Decimal(14,4), 
 SupplierCode varchar(20) 
    )     INSERT INTO @Supplier
    SELECT
        x.c.value('(SupplierId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierName)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(50)'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierNickName)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(50)'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierAddress1)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(100)'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierAddress2)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(100)'),

        x.c.value('(SupplierMobileNo)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20)'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierMobileNo2)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20)'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierGstNo)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20)'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierPanNo)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(20)'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierCityId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierAreaId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierRemarks)[1]', 'NVARCHAR(200)'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierLocation)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierMaxPkno)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierRecordCreated)[1]', 'DATETIME'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierRecordModified)[1]', 'DATETIME'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierUserId)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierLastModified)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierTimeStamp)[1]', 'INT'),
        x.c.value('(SupplierDeActive)[1]', 'BIT'),
       x.c.value('(SupplierGstType)[1]', 'INT'), 
       x.c.value('(SupplierPincode)[1]', 'INT'), 
       x.c.value('(SupplierCreditDays)[1]', 'INT'), 
       x.c.value('(SupplierDiscountPercent)[1]', 'Decimal(14,4)'), 
       x.c.value('(SupplierCode)[1]', 'varchar(20)') 
    FROM @SupplierXML.nodes('/supplier') x(c);


    BEGIN TRY
        IF @SupplierNew = 1
        BEGIN
            INSERT INTO Supplier (
                SupplierName,
                SupplierNickName,
                SupplierAddress1,
                SupplierAddress2,
                SupplierAddress3,
                SupplierEmailID,
                SupplierMobileNo,
                SupplierMobileNo2,
                SupplierGstNo,
                SupplierPanNo,
                SupplierCityId,
                SupplierAreaId,
                SupplierRemarks,
                SupplierLocation,
                SupplierMaxPkno,
                SupplierRecordCreated,
                SupplierRecordModified,
                SupplierUserId,
                SupplierLastModified,
                SupplierDeActive,
                SupplierId,
                SupplierGstType ,
                SupplierPincode, 
                SupplierCreditDays, 
                SupplierDiscountPercent, 
                SupplierCode 

            )
            SELECT
                SupplierName,
                SupplierNickName,
                SupplierAddress1,
                SupplierAddress2,
                SupplierAddress3,
                SupplierEmailID,
                SupplierMobileNo,
                SupplierMobileNo2,
                SupplierGstNo,
                SupplierPanNo,
                SupplierCityId,
                SupplierAreaId,
          SupplierRemarks,
                SupplierLocation,
                SupplierMaxPkno,
                SupplierRecordCreated,
                SupplierRecordModified,
                SupplierUserId,
                SupplierLastModified,
                SupplierDeActive,
                SupplierId,
                SupplierGstType, 
               SupplierPincode, 
               SupplierCreditDays, 
               SupplierDiscountPercent, 
               SupplierCode 

            FROM @Supplier;
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
            DECLARE @ExistingTimeStamp INT;

            SELECT @ExistingTimeStamp = SupplierTimeStamp
            FROM Supplier
            WHERE SupplierId = (SELECT SupplierId FROM @Supplier);

            IF @ExistingTimeStamp IS NULL
            BEGIN
                SET @ErrorMessage = 'Supplier record not found.';
                RETURN;
            END

            IF @ExistingTimeStamp != (SELECT SupplierTimeStamp FROM @Supplier)
            BEGIN
                SET @ErrorMessage = 'The record has been modified by another user.';
                RETURN;
            END

            UPDATE Supplier
            SET
                SupplierName = c.SupplierName,
                SupplierNickName = c.SupplierNickName,
                SupplierAddress1 = c.SupplierAddress1,
                SupplierAddress2 = c.SupplierAddress2,
                SupplierAddress3 = c.SupplierAddress3,
                SupplierEmailID = c.SupplierEmailID,
                SupplierMobileNo = c.SupplierMobileNo,
                SupplierMobileNo2 = c.SupplierMobileNo2,
                SupplierGstNo = c.SupplierGstNo,
                SupplierPanNo = c.SupplierPanNo,
                SupplierCityId = c.SupplierCityId,
                SupplierAreaId = c.SupplierAreaId,
                SupplierRemarks = c.SupplierRemarks,
                SupplierLocation = c.SupplierLocation,
                SupplierMaxPkno = c.SupplierMaxPkno,
                SupplierRecordModified = c.SupplierRecordModified,
                SupplierUserId = c.SupplierUserId,
                SupplierLastModified = c.SupplierLastModified,
                SupplierDeActive = c.SupplierDeActive ,
   			 SupplierGstType =c.SupplierGstType, 
                SupplierPincode =c.SupplierPincode, 
                SupplierDiscountPercent =c.SupplierDiscountPercent,
                SupplierCreditDays =c.SupplierCreditDays, 
                SupplierCode =c.SupplierCode  
            FROM @Supplier c
            WHERE Supplier.SupplierId = c.SupplierId;
        END

        SET @ErrorMessage = NULL;
    END TRY
    BEGIN CATCH
        -- Capture and return the error message
        SET @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE();
         END CATCH   END;

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SaveSupplierBrandList]
                @SupplierBrandListXml XML,
                @SupplierBrandListNew BIT,
                @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000) OUTPUT
            AS
            BEGIN
                SET NOCOUNT ON;
                
                DECLARE @SupplierBrandList TABLE (
                    SupBrId BIGINT,
                    SupbrBrandId BIGINT,
                    Supbrlocation BIGINT,
                    SupbrMaxPkno BIGINT,
                    SupBrSupplierId BIGINT,
                    RecordCreated DATETIME,
                    RecordModified DATETIME,
                    UserId BIGINT,
                    LastModified BIGINT
                );
                
                INSERT INTO @SupplierBrandList
                SELECT
                    T.c.value('(SupBrId)[1]', 'BIGINT') AS SupBrId,
                    T.c.value('(SupbrBrandId)[1]', 'BIGINT') AS SupbrBrandId,
                    T.c.value('(Supbrlocation)[1]', 'BIGINT') AS Supbrlocation,
                    T.c.value('(SupbrMaxPkno)[1]', 'BIGINT') AS SupbrMaxPkno,
                    T.c.value('(SupBrSupplierId)[1]', 'BIGINT') AS SupBrSupplierId,
                    T.c.value('(RecordCreated)[1]', 'DATETIME') AS RecordCreated,
                    T.c.value('(RecordModified)[1]', 'DATETIME') AS RecordModified,
                    T.c.value('(UserId)[1]', 'BIGINT') AS UserId,
                    T.c.value('(LastModified)[1]', 'BIGINT') AS LastModified
                FROM @SupplierBrandListXml.nodes('/supplierbrandlist') AS T(c);
                
                IF @SupplierBrandListNew = 1
                BEGIN
                    INSERT INTO SupplierBrandList (
                        SupBrId, SupbrBrandId, Supbrlocation, SupbrMaxPkno, SupBrSupplierId,
                        RecordCreated, RecordModified, UserId, LastModified
                    )
                    SELECT
                        SupBrId, SupbrBrandId, Supbrlocation, SupbrMaxPkno, SupBrSupplierId,
                        RecordCreated, RecordModified, UserId, LastModified
                    FROM @SupplierBrandList;
                END
                ELSE
                BEGIN
                    UPDATE SupplierBrandList
                    SET
                        SupbrBrandId = s.SupbrBrandId,
                        Supbrlocation = s.Supbrlocation,
                        SupbrMaxPkno = s.SupbrMaxPkno,
                        SupBrSupplierId = s.SupBrSupplierId,
                        RecordModified = s.RecordModified,
                        UserId = s.UserId,
                        LastModified = s.LastModified
                    FROM @SupplierBrandList s
                    WHERE SupplierBrandList.SupBrId = s.SupBrId;
                END
                
                SET @ErrorMessage = NULL;
            END
GO

     isnull(CompanyRateRoundoff ,0) as CompanyRateRound ,isnull(CompanyPanNo ,'') As CompanyPanNo ,isnull(CompanyPincode,0) as CompanyPincode,ISNULL(CompanyEmailId ,'') as CompanyEmailID ,
      Isnull(CompanySourcecodewiseEntry ,0) as CompanySourcecodewiseEntry 	,CompanyFtpUserName,CompanyFtpDetails ,CompanyFtpPassword ,CompanyFtpDirectory, 	
 isnull(CompanyWhatsappUserName,'') As CompanyWhatsappUserName,isnull(CompanyWhatsappToken,'') AS CompanyWhatsappToken,Isnull(CompanyWhatsappMobileNo ,0) As CompanyWhatsappMobileNo ,Isnull(CompanyBillPrintNo,0) As CompanyBillPrintNo,isnull(CompanyDefaultRackNo,0) 	 As CompanyDefaultRackNo, 
 Isnull(CompanyRequireSalesPerson,0) as CompanyRequireSalesPerson,isnull(CompanySendSalesWhatsapp,0) as CompanySendSalesWhatsapp ,Isnull(CompanySendOrderWhatsapp,0) as CompanySendOrderWhatsapp, isnull(CompanyOrderPrintNo ,0) As CompanyOrderPrintNo, 
 isnull(CompanyAllowNegativeEntry ,0) as CompanyAllowNegativeEntry ,isnull(CompanyOrderItemwise,0) as CompanyOrderItemwise,
 isnull(CompanyScanToSaveAndEdit, 0) as CompanyScanToSaveAndEdit,
 isnull(CompanyBillonCredit,0) As CompanyBillonCredit ,isnull(CompanyPhoneNo ,'') as CompanyPhoneNo ,Isnull(CompanyMobileNo ,'') as CompanyMobileNo ,isnull(CompanyAllowQtyInDecimal ,0) As CompanyAllowQtyInDecimal ,
 Isnull(CompanyBarcodeType,0) as CompanyBarcodeType ,ISnull(CompanyUpiId ,'') As CompanyUpiId ,isnull(CompanyBillPrintMessage ,'') As CompanyBillPrintMessage,Isnull(CompanyClientId ,0) As CompanyClientId,Isnull(CompanyPurchaseRoundOff,0) as CompanyPurchaseRoundOff, 
 isnull(CompanyDefaultDiscountPercent,0) As CompanyDefaultDiscountPercent ,isnull(CompanyNegativeSourcecode,'') As CompanyNegativeSourcecode , Isnull(CompanyRequireSubSize,0) as CompanyRequireSubSize,isnull(CompanyCostWoTax ,0) As CompanyCostWoTax,isnull(CompanyWhatsappType,0) As CompanyWhatsappType,isnull(CompanyShowPurchaseMatrixwise,0) As CompanyShowPurchaseMatrixwise,isnull(CompanyPurchaseVerify,0) As CompanyPurchaseVerify,isnull(CompanySalespersonCompulsory ,0) as CompanySalespersonCompulsory, Isnull(CompanySalesmanPointType, 0) As CompanySalesmanPointType, 
 isnull(CompanySmtpHost,'') as CompanySmtpHost, isnull(CompanySmtpPort,0) as CompanySmtpPort, isnull(CompanySmtpEmailId,'') as CompanySmtpEmailId, isnull(CompanyEmailPassword,'') as CompanyEmailPassword, isnull(CompanyEnableSsl,0) as CompanyEnableSsl, isnull(CompanyStockAudit, 0) as CompanyStockAudit, 
 isnull(IsMainCompany, 0) as IsMainCompany, isnull(CompanyType, 0) as CompanyType, isnull(ParentLocation, '') as ParentLocation, isnull(CompanyEnableChargeProvision, 0) as CompanyEnableChargeProvision, isnull(CompanyOpeningStock, 0) as CompanyOpeningStock 
   FROM CompanyProfile
    WHERE CompanyId = @CompanyId
 END
