/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[sp_GetNextPkNo]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetNextPkNo]
    @TableName NVARCHAR(128),         -- Table name as a parameter
    @LocationPrefix NVARCHAR(10),      -- Location prefix (e.g., '101', '102', etc.)
    @PkNoColumn NVARCHAR(128),         -- Column name for PkNo
    @LocationColumn NVARCHAR(128),     -- Column name for location prefix,
	@MaxPknoColumn  NVARCHAR(128),
    @NextPkNo NVARCHAR(20) OUTPUT      -- Output parameter for the next primary key number
AS
BEGIN
    DECLARE @SQL NVARCHAR(MAX);
    DECLARE @MaxPkNo NVARCHAR(20);
    DECLARE @PrefixPattern NVARCHAR(20);

    -- Set the pattern to search for the max PkNo that matches the location prefix
    SET @PrefixPattern = @LocationPrefix + '%';

    -- Construct the dynamic SQL to get the maximum PkNo for the given location prefix
    SET @SQL = N'SELECT @MaxPkNo_OUT = MAX(' + @MaxPknoColumn + ')+1 ' +
               'FROM ' + @TableName + ' ' +
               'WHERE ' + @LocationColumn + ' = @LocationPrefix';

    -- Execute the dynamic SQL with parameter passing to get the max PkNo
    EXEC sp_executesql @SQL,
        N'@MaxPkNo_OUT NVARCHAR(20) OUTPUT, @LocationPrefix NVARCHAR(10)',
        @MaxPkNo_OUT = @MaxPkNo OUTPUT,
        @LocationPrefix = @LocationPrefix;

    -- If no max PkNo was found (first entry for this location), start from the prefix + '001'
    IF @MaxPkNo IS NULL
        SET @NextPkNo = @LocationPrefix +'' + '1';
    ELSE
        -- Generate the next primary key number by incrementing the last found max PkNo
        SET @NextPkNo = @LocationPrefix + @MaxPkNo;
END;

GO

 @NoLastPrintOut BIT = 0, 
 @NoBackdateView BIT = 0, 
 @IsActive BIT = 1, 
 @NoProfitOnDashboard BIT = 0 
 AS 
 BEGIN 
  INSERT INTO master_users (UserName, UserPassword, UserCreated, UserModified, UserRemarks, NoLastPrintOut, NoBackdateView, IsActive, NoProfitOnDashboard) 
 VALUES (@UserName, @UserPassword, GETDATE(), GETDATE(), @UserRemarks, @NoLastPrintOut, @NoBackdateView, @IsActive, @NoProfitOnDashboard); 
 END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[UpdateArea]    Script Date: 11-05-2026 22:35:21 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[UpdateArea] 
    @AreaId BIGINT, 
    @AreaName VARCHAR(50), 
    @AreaRecordModified DATETIME, 
    @AreaLastModified BIGINT, 
    @AreaTimeStamp BIGINT, 
    @AreaZoneId BIGINT 
AS 
BEGIN 
    SET NOCOUNT ON; 

    -- Check if the row has been modified by someone else 
    IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM Area WHERE AreaId = @AreaId AND CAST(AreaTimeStamp AS BIGINT) = @AreaTimeStamp) 
    BEGIN 
        -- Perform the update 
        UPDATE Area 
        SET 
            AreaName = @AreaName, 
            AreaRecordModified = @AreaRecordModified, 
            AreaLastModified = @AreaLastModified, 
            AreaZoneId = @AreaZoneId 
        WHERE AreaId = @AreaId; 
    END 
    ELSE 
    BEGIN 
        -- Return an error code if there was a concurrency conflict 
        RAISERROR ('Record has been modified by another user.', 16, 1); 
    END 
END;
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON

Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[UpdateBrand] 
       @BrandId BIGINT,
       @BrandName VARCHAR(50),
       @BrandRecordModified DATETIME,
       @BrandLastModified BIGINT,
       @BrandTimeStamp Bigint
   AS
   BEGIN
       SET NOCOUNT ON;
      IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM Brand WHERE Brandid = @BrandId and Cast(BrandTimeStamp As Bigint )= @BrandTimeStamp)
       BEGIN
           UPDATE Brand
           SET BrandName = @BrandName,
               BrandRecordModified = @BrandRecordModified,
               BrandLastModified = @BrandLastModified
           WHERE BrandId = @BrandId ;
       END
       ELSE
       BEGIN 
         RAISERROR ('Record has been modified by another user.', 16, 1);  
       END
   END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[UpdateCategory] 
 @CategoryId BIGINT,
 @CategoryCode VARCHAR(30),
 @CategoryDescription VARCHAR(50),
 @CategoryRecordModified DATETIME,
 @CategoryLastModified BIGINT,
 @CategoryTimeStamp BIGINT,
 @CategoryDeptId BIGINT,
 @CategoryHsnId BIGINT,
 @CategorySizeId BIGINT,
 @CategoryDeactive BIT
 AS
 BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
    -- Check if the row has been modified by someone else
    IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM Category WHERE Categoryid = @CategoryId AND CAST(CategoryTimeStamp AS BIGINT) = @CategoryTimeStamp)
    BEGIN
        -- Perform the update
        UPDATE Category
        SET CategoryDescription = @CategoryDescription,
            CategoryCode = @CategoryCode,
            CategoryRecordModified = @CategoryRecordModified,
            CategoryLastModified = @CategoryLastModified,
            CategoryDeptID = @CategoryDeptId,
            CategoryHsnId = @CategoryHsnId,
            CategorySizeId = @CategorySizeId,
            CategoryDeactive = @CategoryDeactive
        WHERE CategoryId = @CategoryId;
    END
    ELSE
    BEGIN
        -- Return an error code if there was a concurrency conflict
        RAISERROR ('Record has been modified by another user.', 16, 1);
    END
 END;
GO

  Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[UpdateCharge] 
 @ChargeId BIGINT,
 @ChargeDesc VARCHAR(30),
 	@ChargeRate decimal(14,4),
    @ChargeRecordModified DATETIME,
     @ChargeLastModified BIGINT,
 	@ChargeTimeStamp Bigint 
 AS
 BEGIN 
     SET NOCOUNT ON; 
 
     IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM ChargeMaster WHERE Chargeid = @ChargeId and Cast(ChargeTimeStamp As Bigint )= @ChargeTimeStamp)
     BEGIN 
        UPDATE ChargeMaster 
        SET ChargeDesc = @ChargeDesc, 
 ChargeRate=@ChargeRate, 
 ChargeRecordModified = @ChargeRecordModified, 
 ChargeLastModified = @ChargeLastModified 
 WHERE ChargeId = @ChargeId ; 
 END 
 ELSE 
 BEGIN 
  RAISERROR ('Record has been modified by another user.', 16, 1);   
 END 
 END

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[UpdateCity] 
    @CityId BIGINT, 
    @CityName VARCHAR(50), 
    @CityRecordModified DATETIME, 
    @CityLastModified BIGINT, 
    @CityTimeStamp BIGINT, 
    @CityStateId BIGINT 
AS 
BEGIN 
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Check if the row has been modified by someone else
    IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM City WHERE CityId = @CityId AND CAST(CityTimeStamp AS BIGINT) = @CityTimeStamp) 
    BEGIN 
        -- Perform the update
        UPDATE City 
        SET 
            CityName = @CityName, 
            CityRecordModified = @CityRecordModified, 
            CityLastModified = @CityLastModified, 
            CityStateId = @CityStateId 
        WHERE 
            CityId = @CityId;
    END 
    ELSE 
    BEGIN

    @DeptTimeStamp BIGINT, 
    @DeptDeactive BIT 
AS 
BEGIN 
    SET NOCOUNT ON; 

    -- Check if the row has been modified by someone else 
    IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM Department WHERE DeptId = @DeptId AND CAST(DeptTimeStamp AS BIGINT) = @DeptTimeStamp) 
    BEGIN

        RETURN; 
    END

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[UpdateState] 
    @StateId BIGINT, 
    @StateName VARCHAR(50), 
    @StateRecordModified DATETIME, 
    @StateLastModified BIGINT, 
    @StateTimeStamp BIGINT, 
    @StateCountryId BIGINT, 
    @StateGstCode VARCHAR(10),
    @StateUT Bit 
AS 
BEGIN 
    SET NOCOUNT ON; 

    -- Check if the row has been modified by someone else 
    IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM States WHERE StateId = @StateId AND CAST(StateTimeStamp AS BIGINT) = @StateTimeStamp) 
    BEGIN 
        -- Perform the update 
        UPDATE States 
        SET StateName = @StateName, 
            StateRecordModified = @StateRecordModified, 
            StateLastModified = @StateLastModified, 
            StateCountryId = @StateCountryId, 
            StateGstCode = @StateGstCode, 
            StateUT = @StateUT 
        WHERE StateId = @StateId; 
    END 
    ELSE 
    BEGIN 
        -- Prepare the error message with line breaks 
        DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000); 
        SET @ErrorMessage = 'Record has been modified by another user.' + CHAR(13) + CHAR(10) + 
                            'Please reload the data and try again.'; 

        -- Raise the error 
        RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, 16, 1); 
    END 
END
GO

 AS

 BEGIN 
 UPDATE TaxMaster

 TaxRate =@TaxRate, 
 TaxCgst =@TaxCgst, 
 TaxSgst =@TaxSgst, 
 TaxIgst =@TaxIgst, 
 TaxUgst =@TaxUgst, 
 TaxType=@TaxType,

Create PROCEDURE [dbo].[UpdateUser] 
    @UserId BIGINT, 
    @UserName VARCHAR(50), 
    @UserPassword VARCHAR(256), 
    @UserModified DATETIME, 
    @UserRemarks NVARCHAR(256), 
    @NoLastPrintOut BIT = 0, 
    @NoBackdateView BIT = 0, 
    @IsActive BIT = 1, 
    @NoProfitOnDashboard BIT = 0 
AS 
BEGIN 
    SET NOCOUNT ON; 

    -- Check if the row has been modified by someone else 
    IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM Master_Users WHERE UserId = @UserId) 
    BEGIN 
        -- Perform the update 
        UPDATE Master_Users 
        SET UserName = @UserName, 
            UserPassword = @UserPassword, 
            UserModified = @UserModified, 
            UserRemarks = @UserRemarks, 
            NoLastPrintOut = @NoLastPrintOut, 
            NoBackdateView = @NoBackdateView, 
            IsActive = @IsActive, 
            NoProfitOnDashboard = @NoProfitOnDashboard 
        WHERE UserId = @UserId; 
    END 
    ELSE 
    BEGIN 
        -- Return an error code if there was a concurrency conflict 
        RAISERROR('Record has been modified or does not exist.', 16, 1); 
    END 
END;

SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[usp_GetAllCustomers]
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    SELECT 
        CustomerId,
        CustomerName,
        CustomerNickName,
        CustomerAddress1,
        CustomerAddress2,
        CustomerAddress3,
        CustomerEmailID,
        CustomerMobileNo,
        CustomerMobileNo2,
        CustomerGstNo,
        CustomerPanNo,
        CustomerBirthDate,
        CustomerAnnDate,
        CustomerCityId,
        CustomerAreaId,
        CustomerRemarks,
        CustomerLocation,
        CustomerMaxPkno,
        CustomerRecordCreated,
        CustomerRecordModified,
        CustomerUserId,
        CustomerLastModified,
        CustomerTimeStamp
    FROM 
        Customer;
END;
